REL-REF    (O,41298001,A.Filatenkov+,R,RI-252,1999)               41240  1   43 
COMMENT    Of author V.Filatenkov, received 29 March 2013 by      41240  1   44 
           S.Simakov (NDS IAEA), forwarded to CJD 6 April 2013:   41240  1   45 
           "27Al(n,a) cs were taken from the evaluation EAF-4 of  41240  1   46 
           that time.Some explanations should be done to this.    41240  1   47 
           1.  In reality, all the cross sections were measured in41240  1   48 
           our experiments relatively to the 93Nb(n,2n) c-s (if   41240  1   49 
           other was not pointed out specially).                  41240  1   50 
           2.  However, this cross section that is very convenient41240  1   51 
           for practical use was not evaluated good enough at that41240  1   52 
           time.                                                  41240  1   53 
           3.  We decided to improve the data of 93Nb(n,2n) using 41240  1   54 
           the ratio of 27Al(n,a) to 93Nb(n,2n) cs measured in the41240  1   55 
           large body of our experiments. This ratio is shown in  41240  1   56 
           Fig. 2.2 of ref. RI-252.                               41240  1   57 
           4.  The corrected in such a way data of 93Nb(n,2n) were41240  1   58 
           finally used as the reference cross section in our     41240  1   59 
           measurements.                                          41240  1   60 
           So, in fact, all the data of our measurements are first41240  1   61 
           related to the 27Al(n,a) cross section.                41240  1   62 
           However, it would be not quite correctly to write this,41240  1   63 
           because Al foils were used often, but not in every     41240  1   64 
           measurement. In the contrary, the niobium foils were   41240  1   65 
           used ALWAYS, and namely the 93Nb(n,2n) c-s was used in 41240  1   66 
           calculations.THE ONE CORRECTED BY US.                  41240  1   67 
           This is why the both cross sections, the 27Al(n,a) and 41240  1   68 
           the 93Nb(n,2n) were given in our works as reference    41240  1   69 
           ones.                                                  41240  1   70 
           Probably, it would be better to give in the            41240  1   71 
           corresponding Tables of our works three column:        41240  1   72 
           1.  The 27Al(n,a) data taken from the evaluation       41240  1   73 
           2.  The 93Nb(n,2n) to 27Al(n,a) ratio measured by us   41240  1   74 
           3.  The corrected 93Nb(n,2n) cs that is the result of  41240  1   75 
           multiplication of the evaluated 27Al(n,a) data by the  41240  1   76 
           measured ratio, it means the data that were finally    41240  1   77 
           used in our measurements as the reference c-s.         41240  1   78 
           ----------                                             41240  1   79 
           Of compiler M.M.                                       41240  1   80 
           Question was sent to V.Filatenkov 08 April 2013:       41240  1   81 
           A question concerning the sentence:                    41240  1   82 
           >   1.  The 27Al(n,a) data taken from the evaluation.  41240  1   83 
           Does it mean, that all 15 points for Al(n,a) c-s were  41240  1   84 
           obtained from interpolation of EAF-4 ?                 41240  1   85 
           Or only part of them?                                  41240  1   86 
           I ask, because as clearly see on Fig.2.2 of            41240  1   87 
           R,INDC-CCP-0402 (in attached file; data given for      41240  1   88 
           Al(n,a) c-s in INDC-CCP-0402 and RI-252 are the same), 41240  1   89 
           only 9 lower (in En region) points lie directly on     41240  1   90 
           EAF-4 curve, but for 6 upper (in En) points there are  41240  1   91 
           some visual deviation from EAF-4.                      41240  1   92 
           Could you please comment these deviations from EAF-4 ? 41240  1   93 
           May be, not all given points were from EAF, but only   41240  1   94 
           several lower points ?                                 41240  1   95 
           And also, we would appreciate greatly, if you could be 41240  1   96 
           so kind to send us the directly measured ratio         41240  1   97 
           Nb(n,2n)/Al(n,a) c-s, given on Fig. 2.2 of RI-252 as   41240  1   98 
           primarily measured data.                               41240  1   99
